< text>
When Leucadia Pizzeria opened the Vista location, my family was ecstatic! My kids LOVE the calzone options, and the pizza, pasta, and garlic bread is the best! Wait times can be a little long in the evenings, best to order ahead if possible on a Friday, Saturday or Sunday night. The owner is an amazing human being, and she LOVES her customers and it shows. I had an issue with an order one Saturday night, and she called me personally to work out the details and make sure everything was perfect. We will continue to be fans, and will recommend to all of our friends and family. Try them out, you'll be SO glad you did! Try the lobster pizza or the lobster mac, it's seriously amazing!</text>

I love ice cream. What I love most about Baskin-robbins is the 31 flavors I get to choose from. This BK has been in Redlands as long as I can remember. The employees are always friendly, and the service is top notch. There is very little seating inside (4 two-person tables) but there are at least 8 benches, with shade, on the corner outside. < Review>
Lido Cafe and Bakery has been in the neighborhood  a long time! Shawna has moved into a bigger space with sole focus on the restaurant. The restaurant serves breakfast and lunch, and offers a dinner menu  Wednesday thru Sunday. Check the website for specifics. My family enjoyed Easter brunch at Lido and we were quite happy with our meal. We ordered Strawberry French Toast,  Country Fried Steak and a Turkey Bacon Avocado sandwich. Everything was very tasty! The service staff looked great and was very attentive! Our server, Gustavo,  was GREAT! There is a bakery display of beautiful pastries that greets you as you arrive. You'll be full when you leave, so order them to take home!< /Review>

IF I COULD 4.5 STARS!!!!!! ^-^

I came to this cafe and I was greeted with a warm smile and I loved their hospitality, especially Shauna! She handled and tended to my needs whenever she had the time, especially when I was the only guest while everyone else came in as parties of two or more. We went there at 7:45pm on Sat. There were perhaps 8 other diners in the restuarant,  plus us. Dinner salads are small and skimpy, as if there is a lettuce shortage or perhaps they believe lettuce is the price of gold. There were only 8-10 small chopped pieces of tomato and 4 croutons.
